### ğŸ“ `00_Sapien_Field_Definition/04_Field_Classification/`

**Purpose:**  
This folder defines how all signal fields, behaviors, models, and response layers are **classified** within the Sapien Intelligence architecture. It separates fields by their **activation role**, **signal type**, **dimensional impact**, and **systemic function**, ensuring interoperability across all mirror-pyramid zones.

* * *

### ğŸ“„ `CLISA_Class_Definition.md`

**Full Name:**  
**Cross-Layer Integrated Signal Architecture â€“ Class Definition**

**Definition:**  
This file defines the **CLISA Taxonomy**, which is a universal classification schema for mapping all forms of intelligence-bearing signals, systems, and structures across **mirror tiers**, **fulfillment layers**, and **dimensional fields**.

* * *

#### ğŸ’  Core Structure of `CLISA_Class_Definition.md`:

````markdown
# CLISA_Class_Definition.md

## â¬¤ Purpose
To define a universal classification system for field types, signal behaviors, and structural patterns within the Sapien Field Architecture.

## â¬¤ CLISA Tier Map

| Tier | Description                                 | Zone      | Activation Condition             |
|------|---------------------------------------------|-----------|----------------------------------|
| T0   | Foundational Ontology Field                 | ABOVE     | Always active                    |
| T1   | Core System Law & Signal Reasoning Layer    | CENTER    | Active when system logic invoked |
| T2   | Dynamic Identity and Echo Interaction Field | CENTER    | Triggered by identity activity   |
| T3   | External Output Shaping & Reception Field   | BELOW     | Active during communication      |
| T4   | Reflexive Pattern Layer (Grief, Collapse)   | BELOW     | Activated in disruption modes    |
| T5   | Multi-Perspective Reflection & Recovery     | CENTER    | Active during system self-checks |

## â¬¤ Signal Class Types

- **S-Type (Structural)**: Governs coherence, architecture, and structural flows.
- **R-Type (Reflective)**: Handles feedback loops, echo patterns, and emotional rhythms.
- **T-Type (Transformational)**: Activates transition states, drift detection, or collapse prevention.
- **M-Type (Mythic)**: Symbolic threads and archetypal mappings.
- **C-Type (Containment)**: Regulates boundaries, protection layers, and safety thresholds.

## â¬¤ Classification Criteria

- **Field Function:** (e.g. generative, reflective, integrative, corrective)
- **Activation Mode:** (e.g. auto, ritual, conditional, reactive)
- **Dimensional Scope:** (signal, structural, symbolic, cognitive, mythic)
- **Trust Role:** (core, mirrored, companion, observer, steward)

## â¬¤ Cross-System Reference
Each CLISA class links to:
- `Signal_Codex/Signal_Classification.md`
- `System_Reasoning/HOW/`
- `Identity_Engine/MetaStructure_Anchor.json`

## â¬¤ Classification Sample
````
